# Text Elements
F(A-B) = g(B) + h(B)
=1+4
=5 ^n3tGjq0I

F(n) = g(n)+h(n) ^k03WLpLW

F(A-C-D) = g(C)+h(C)+g(d)+h(D)
=1+2+1+3
=7 ^ocEzTa9D

F(A-3) = g(B) + h(B)
=1+4
=5 ^DtbvAd4V

F(B-E) = 1+6 = 7
F(B-F) = 1+8 = 9  ^5syRJxn1

F(C-G) = 1+2 = 3
F(C-H-I) = 1+0+0+1 = 2
F(D-J) = 1+0 = 1 ^2JVQ7VMc

Solution : 
- 1st path => ABE 
=> 6+1+4+1 = 12
- 2nd path => ACJ-ACH-ACI
=> 2+2+(1+3)+2
=> 2 + 3 + 4 +2 
=> 10  ^fYAj0tgb
